## Is your feature request related to a problem? Please describe.

I am writing a chezmoi script that will prompt the user whether they want to restore or create a GPG key.

That script, however, should not execute when the stdin is not interactive (like in scripts or docker containers).

The `stdinIsATTY` function serves that purpose well, but I can only use it during init.

## Describe the solution you'd like

It would be nice if `stdinIsATTY` was available to all templates, beyond just init.

## Describe alternatives you've considered

I can check that within the script itself, like `test -t 0` in Bash.

## Additional context

N/A

   928	// createConfigFileContents creates a config file using a template and returns
   929	// its contents.
   930	func (c *Config) createConfigFileContents(filename chezmoi.RelPath, data []byte, cmd *cobra.Command) ([]byte, error) {
   931	        // Clone funcMap and restore it after creating the config.
   932	        // This ensures that the init template functions
   933	        // are removed before "normal" template parsing.
   934	        funcMap := make(template.FuncMap)
   935	        chezmoi.RecursiveMerge(funcMap, c.templateFuncs)
   936	        defer func() {
   937	                c.templateFuncs = funcMap
   938	        }()
   939	
   940	        initTemplateFuncs := map[string]any{
   941	                "exit":                  c.exitInitTemplateFunc,
   942	                "promptBool":            c.promptBoolInteractiveTemplateFunc,
   943	                "promptBoolOnce":        c.promptBoolOnceInteractiveTemplateFunc,
   944	                "promptChoice":          c.promptChoiceInteractiveTemplateFunc,
   945	                "promptChoiceOnce":      c.promptChoiceOnceInteractiveTemplateFunc,
   946	                "promptInt":             c.promptIntInteractiveTemplateFunc,
   947	                "promptIntOnce":         c.promptIntOnceInteractiveTemplateFunc,
   948	                "promptMultichoice":     c.promptMultichoiceInteractiveTemplateFunc,
   949	                "promptMultichoiceOnce": c.promptMultichoiceOnceInteractiveTemplateFunc,
   950	                "promptString":          c.promptStringInteractiveTemplateFunc,
   951	                "promptStringOnce":      c.promptStringOnceInteractiveTemplateFunc,
   952	                "stdinIsATTY":           c.stdinIsATTYInitTemplateFunc,
   953	                "writeToStdout":         c.writeToStdout,
   954	        }
   955	        chezmoi.RecursiveMerge(c.templateFuncs, initTemplateFuncs)
   956	
   957	        tmpl, err := chezmoi.ParseTemplate(filename.String(), data, chezmoi.TemplateOptions{
   958	                Funcs:   c.templateFuncs,
   959	                Options: slices.Clone(c.Template.Options),
   960	        })
   961	        if err != nil {
   962	                return nil, err
   963	        }
   964	
   965	        templateData := c.getTemplateDataMap(cmd)
   966	        if c.init.data {
   967	                chezmoi.RecursiveMerge(templateData, c.Data)
   968	        }
   969	        return tmpl.Execute(templateData)
   970	}

    11	func (c *Config) exitInitTemplateFunc(code int) string {

    15	func (c *Config) stdinIsATTYInitTemplateFunc() bool {
    16	        if c.noTTY {
    17	                return false
    18	        }
    19	        file, ok := c.stdin.(*os.File)
    20	        if !ok {
    21	                return false
    22	        }
    23	        return term.IsTerminal(int(file.Fd()))
    24	}

    67	func (c *Config) runExecuteTemplateCmd(cmd *cobra.Command, args []string) error {
    68	        options := []chezmoi.SourceStateOption{
    69	                chezmoi.WithTemplateDataOnly(true),
    70	                chezmoi.WithReadTemplates(!c.executeTemplate.init),
    71	        }
    72	        if c.executeTemplate.init {
    73	                options = append(options, chezmoi.WithReadTemplateData(false))
    74	        }
    75	        if c.executeTemplate.withStdin && len(args) > 0 {
    76	                stdin, err := io.ReadAll(c.stdin)
    77	                if err != nil {
    78	                        return err
    79	                }
    80	                options = append(options, chezmoi.WithPriorityTemplateData(map[string]any{
    81	                        "chezmoi": map[string]any{
    82	                                "stdin": string(stdin),
    83	                        },
    84	                }))
    85	        }
    86	        sourceState, err := c.newSourceState(cmd.Context(), cmd, options...)
    87	        if err != nil {
    88	                return err
    89	        }

    67	func (c *Config) promptBoolInteractiveTemplateFunc(prompt string, args ...bool) bool {
    68	        if len(args) > 1 {
    69	                panic(fmt.Errorf("want 1 or 2 arguments, got %d", len(args)+1))
    70	        }
    71	
    72	        if valueStr, ok := c.interactiveTemplateFuncs.promptBool[prompt]; ok {
    73	                return mustValue(chezmoi.ParseBool(valueStr))
    74	        }
    75	
    76	        return mustValue(c.promptBool(prompt, args...))
    77	}
    78	
    79	func (c *Config) promptBoolOnceInteractiveTemplateFunc(m map[string]any, path any, prompt string, args ...bool) bool {
    80	        if len(args) > 1 {
    81	                panic(fmt.Errorf("want 3 or 4 arguments, got %d", len(args)+2))
    82	        }
    83	
    84	        nestedMap, lastKey := mustValues(nestedMapAtPath(m, path))
    85	        if !c.interactiveTemplateFuncs.forcePromptOnce {
    86	                if value, ok := nestedMap[lastKey]; ok {
    87	                        switch value := value.(type) {
    88	                        case bool:
    89	                                return value
    90	                        case string:
    91	                                if boolValue, err := chezmoi.ParseBool(value); err == nil {
    92	                                        return boolValue
    93	                                }
    94	                        }
    95	                }
    96	        }
    97	
    98	        return c.promptBoolInteractiveTemplateFunc(prompt, args...)
    99	}
   100	
   101	func (c *Config) promptChoiceInteractiveTemplateFunc(prompt string, choices any, args ...string) string {
   102	        if len(args) > 1 {
   103	                panic(fmt.Errorf("want 2 or 3 arguments, got %d", len(args)+2))
   104	        }
   105	
   106	        if valueStr, ok := c.interactiveTemplateFuncs.promptChoice[prompt]; ok {
   107	                return valueStr
   108	        }
   109	
   110	        choiceStrs := mustValue(anyToStringSlice(choices))
   111	        return mustValue(c.promptChoice(prompt, choiceStrs, args...))
   112	}
   113	
   114	func (c *Config) promptChoiceOnceInteractiveTemplateFunc(
   115	        m map[string]any,
   116	        path any,
   117	        prompt string,
   118	        choices any,
   119	        args ...string,
   120	) string {
   121	        if len(args) > 1 {
   122	                panic(fmt.Errorf("want 4 or 5 arguments, got %d", len(args)+4))
   123	        }
   124	
   125	        nestedMap, lastKey := mustValues(nestedMapAtPath(m, path))
   126	        if !c.interactiveTemplateFuncs.forcePromptOnce {
   127	                if value, ok := nestedMap[lastKey]; ok {
   128	                        if valueStr, ok := value.(string); ok {
   129	                                return valueStr
   130	                        }
   131	                }
   132	        }
   133	
   134	        return c.promptChoiceInteractiveTemplateFunc(prompt, choices, args...)
   135	}
   136	
   137	func (c *Config) promptMultichoiceInteractiveTemplateFunc(prompt string, choices any, args ...any) []string {
   138	        if len(args) > 1 {
   139	                panic(fmt.Errorf("want 2 or 3 arguments, got %d", len(args)+2))
   140	        }
   141	
   142	        if valueStr, ok := c.interactiveTemplateFuncs.promptMultichoice[prompt]; ok {
   143	                return strings.Split(valueStr, "/")
   144	        }
   145	
   146	        choiceStrs := mustValue(anyToStringSlice(choices))
   147	
   148	        var defaultValue *[]string
   149	
   150	        if len(args) == 1 && args[0] != nil {
   151	                values := mustValue(anyToStringSlice(args[0]))
   152	                defaultValue = &values
   153	        }
   154	
   155	        return mustValue(c.promptMultichoice(prompt, choiceStrs, defaultValue))
   156	}
   157	
   158	func (c *Config) promptMultichoiceOnceInteractiveTemplateFunc(
   159	        m map[string]any,
   160	        path any,
   161	        prompt string,
   162	        choices any,
   163	        args ...any,
   164	) []string {
   165	        if len(args) > 1 {
   166	                panic(fmt.Errorf("want 4 or 5 arguments, got %d", len(args)+4))
   167	        }
   168	
   169	        nestedMap, lastKey := mustValues(nestedMapAtPath(m, path))
   170	        if !c.interactiveTemplateFuncs.forcePromptOnce {
   171	                if value, ok := nestedMap[lastKey]; ok {
   172	                        return mustValue(anyToStringSlice(value))
   173	                }
   174	        }
   175	
   176	        return c.promptMultichoiceInteractiveTemplateFunc(prompt, choices, args...)
   177	}
   178	
   179	func (c *Config) promptIntInteractiveTemplateFunc(prompt string, args ...int64) int64 {
   180	        if len(args) > 1 {
   181	                panic(fmt.Errorf("want 1 or 2 arguments, got %d", len(args)+1))
   182	        }
   183	
   184	        if value, ok := c.interactiveTemplateFuncs.promptInt[prompt]; ok {
   185	                return int64(value)
   186	        }
   187	
   188	        return mustValue(c.promptInt(prompt, args...))
   189	}

   192	        if len(args) > 1 {

   203	        }
   204	
   205	        return c.promptIntInteractiveTemplateFunc(prompt, args...)

    71	func (c *Config) commentTemplateFunc(prefix, s string) string {
    72	        var builder strings.Builder
    73	        for line := range strings.Lines(s) {
    74	                builder.WriteString(prefix)
    75	                builder.WriteString(line)

    80	func (c *Config) deleteValueAtPathTemplateFunc(path string, dict map[string]any) any {
    81	        keys, lastKey := mustValues(keysFromPath(path))
    82	        currentMap := dict
    83	        for _, key := range keys {
    84	                value, ok := currentMap[key]
    85	                if !ok {
    86	                        return dict
    87	                }
    88	                nestedMap, ok := value.(map[string]any)
    89	                if !ok {
    90	                        return dict
    91	                }
    92	                currentMap = nestedMap
    93	        }
    94	        delete(currentMap, lastKey)
    95	
    96	        return dict
    97	}

   102	        }
   103	        for _, s := range more {
   104	                if strings.EqualFold(first, s) {
   105	                        return true
   106	                }
   107	        }
   108	        return false
   109	}

   627	// to c. It panics if there is already an existing template function with the

   630	        if _, ok := c.templateFuncs[key]; ok {

     1	# `execute-template` [*template*...]
     2	
     3	Execute *template*s. This is useful for [testing templates][testing] or for
     4	calling chezmoi from other scripts. *templates* are interpreted as literal
     5	templates, with no whitespace added to the output between arguments. If no
     6	templates are specified, the template is read from stdin.
     7	
     8	## Flags
     9	
    10	### `-f`, `--file`
    11	
    12	Treat the arguments as filenames, not literal templates.
    13	
    14	### `-i`, `--init`
    15	
    16	Include simulated functions only available during `chezmoi init`.
    17

    19	
    20	Set the left template delimiter.
    21	
    22	### `--promptBool` *pairs*
    23	
    24	Simulate the `promptBool` template function with a function that returns values
    25	from *pairs*. *pairs* is a comma-separated list of *prompt*`=`*value* pairs. If
    26	`promptBool` is called with a *prompt* that does not match any of *pairs*, then
    27	it returns false.
    28	
    29	### `--promptChoice` *pairs*
    30	
    31	Simulate the `promptChoice` template function with a function that returns
    32	values from *pairs*. *pairs* is a comma-separated list of *prompt*`=`*value*
    33	pairs. If `promptChoice` is called with a *prompt* that does not match any of
    34	*pairs*, then it returns *prompt* unchanged.
    35	
    36	### `--promptInt` *pairs*

    38	Simulate the `promptInt` template function with a function that returns values

    40	`promptInt` is called with a *prompt* that does not match any of *pairs*, then

     1	package chezmoi
     2	
     3	// recursiveCopy returns a recursive copy of v.
     4	func recursiveCopy(v any) any {
     5	        m, ok := v.(map[string]any)
     6	        if !ok {
     7	                return v
     8	        }
     9	        c := make(map[string]any)
    10	        for key, value := range m {
    11	                if mapValue, ok := value.(map[string]any); ok {
    12	                        c[key] = recursiveCopy(mapValue)
    13	                } else {
    14	                        c[key] = value
    15	                }
    16	        }
    17	        return c
    18	}
    19	
    20	// RecursiveMerge recursively merges maps in source into dest.
    21	func RecursiveMerge(dest, source map[string]any) {
    22	        for key, sourceValue := range source {
    23	                destValue, ok := dest[key]
    24	                if !ok {
    25	                        dest[key] = recursiveCopy(sourceValue)
    26	                        continue
    27	                }
    28	                destMap, ok := destValue.(map[string]any)
    29	                if !ok || destMap == nil {
    30	                        dest[key] = recursiveCopy(sourceValue)
    31	                        continue
    32	                }
    33	                sourceMap, ok := sourceValue.(map[string]any)
    34	                if !ok {
    35	                        dest[key] = recursiveCopy(sourceValue)
    36	                        continue
    37	                }
    38	                RecursiveMerge(destMap, sourceMap)
    39	        }
    40	}
    41
